   vyākīrṇaṃ vākyasaṃkīrṇamapūrṇaṃ vākyagarbhitam // ViPrud_5.20 //	vyAkIrNam vAkya saMkIrNam apUrNam vAkya garBitam // ViPrut _5.20 //
   dve bhinnaliṅgavacane dve ca nyūnādhikopame /	dve Binna liFga vacane dve ca nyUna aDika upame /
   bhagnacchando yatibhraṣṭamaśarīramarītikam // ViPrud_5.21 //	Bagna= CandaH yati Brazwam aSarIra marItikam // ViPrut _5.21 //
   visargaluptamasthānasamāsaṃ vācyavarjitam /	visarga luptam asTAna samAsam vAcya varjitam /
   samāptapunarāttaṃ ca tathā saṃbandhavarjitam // ViPrud_5.22 //	samApta punar Attam ca taTA saMbanDa varjitam // ViPrut _5.22 //
   patatprakarṣamadhikapadaṃ prakramabhaṅgavat /	patat prakarzam aDika padam prakrama BaFga vat /
   caturviṃśatirucyante doṣā vākyasamāśritāḥ // ViPrud_5.23 //	caturviMSatiH ucyante dozAH vAkya samASritAH // ViPrut _5.23 //
   eṣāṃ svarūpamudāharaṇaṃ ca /	ezAm svarUpam udAharaNam ca /
   [V.3.1 śabdahīnam]	[V.3.1  Sabda hInam]
   śabdaśāstrahataṃ vākyaṃ śabdahīnaṃ prakīrtyate /	Sabda SAstra hatam vAkyam Sabda hInam prakIrtyate /
   yathā śatruvākyeṣu   	yaTA Satru vAkyezu   
   na saṃśṛṇumahe hanta hitamāptairnimantritam /	na saMSRNumahe hanta hitam AptEH nimantritam /
   yena kākatibhūbhartuḥ sevāṃ hitvā hatā vayam // ViPrud_5.24 //	yena kAkatiBU BartuH sevAm hitvA hatAH vayam // ViPrut _5.24 //
   atra hitaṃ na saṃśṛṇumahe iti padadvayaprayoge doṣāviṣkārādvākyameva	atra hitam na saMSRNumahe iti pada dvaya prayoge doza AvizkArAt vAkyam eva
   duṣṭamiti na padadoṣaśaṅkā /	duzwam iti na pada doza SaFkA /
   saṃpūrvasya śṛṇoterātmanepaditve karmaṇo 'nupādānaniyamāt /	saMpUrvasya SRNoteH AtmanA Ipaditve karmaNaH anupAdAna niyamAt /
   atha kramabhraṣṭam /	aTa krama Brazwam /
   kramabhraṣṭaṃ bhavedārthaḥ śābdo vā yatra na kramaḥ // ViPrud_5.25 //	krama Brazwam Bavet ArTaH SAbdaH vA yatra na kramaH // ViPrut _5.25 //
   [V.3.2 kramabhraṣṭam]	[V.3.2 kram aBrazwam]
   yathā   	yaTA   
   prabhave kākatīndrāya turagān kariṇo 'thavā /	praBave kAkati indrAya turagAn kariNaH aTavA /

   atra kariṇo yadvā turagāniti vaktavye vyutkrameṇoktam, turagāpekṣayā	atra kariNaH yat vA turagAn iti vaktavye vyutkrameNa uktam, turaga apekzayA
   kariṇāmutkṛṣṭatvāt /	kariNAm utkRzwa tvAt /

   śabdakramabhaṅgo yathā   	Sabda krama BaFgaH yaTA   
   kā nāma gaṇanāsmāsu kākatīyasya bhūpateḥ /	kA nAma gaNanA asmAsu kAkatIyasya BUpateH /
   yaśaḥ pratāpayormagnau sūryācandramasāvapi // ViPrud_5.27 //	yaSaH pratApayoH magnO sUryAcandramasO= api // ViPrut _5.27 //

   yaśaḥ pratāpayoḥ sūryācandramasau magnāviti samudāyadvayānvaye	yaSaH pratApayoH sUryAcandramasO magnO= iti samudAya dvaya anvaye
   yathāyogyamarthānvaye siddhe nārthakramavirodhaḥ /	yaTAyogyam arTa anvaye sidDe na arTa krama viroDaH /
   api tu śabdaprayoga eva kramabhaṅgaḥ /	api tu Sabda prayogaH eva krama BaFgaH /
   [V.3.3 visandhi]	[V.3.3 visanDi]

   [V.3.6 vākyasaṃkīrṇam]	[V.3.6  vAkya saMkIrNam]

   [V.3.7 apūrṇam]	[V.3.7 a pUrNam]

   yathā   	yaTA

   [VI.1 guṇānāmudeśaḥ]	[VI.1 guNAn AmudeSaH]
   eṣāṃ madhye keṣāṃcid doṣaparihārakatvena guṇatvam / keṣāṃcit svata	ezAm maDye kezAMcid doza parihAraka tvena guNa tvam / kezAMcid svata
   evotkarṣahetutvād guṇatvam / tatra ye svata eva cārutvātiśayahetavaste	eva utkarza hetu tvAt guNa tvam / tatra ye svatas eva cArutvA atiSaya hetavaH te
   paramutkṛṣṭāḥ / duṣṭatvaparihārahetūnāṃ guṇatvaṃ na sarvasaṃmatam / ye tu	param utkRzwAH / duzwa tva parihAra hetUnAm guNa tvam na sarva saMmatam / ye tu
   doṣābhāvatayā guṇatvamicchanti teṣāmeva saukumāryādayo guṇatvena saṃmatāḥ	doza aBAva tayA guNa tvam icCanti tezAm eva sOkumArya AdayaH guNa tvena saMmatAH
   / śrutikaṭurūpadoṣanirākaraṇāya saukumāryaṃ saṃmatam /	/ Sruti kawu rUpa doza nirAkaraNAya sOkumAryam saMmatam /
   grāmyadoṣanirākaraṇāya kāntiḥ svīkṛtā /	grAmya doza nirAkaraNAya kAntiH svIkRtA /
   apuṣṭārthanirākaraṇāyārthavyaktirmatā / nyūnādhikapadanirākaraṇāya	apuzwa arTa nirAkaraNAya arTa vyaktiH matA / nyUna aDika pada nirAkaraNAya
   saṃmitatvaṃ matam / anucitārthanirākaraṇārthamudāttatā svīkṛtā /	saMmita tvam matam / anucita arTa nirAkaraNa arTam udAtta tA svIkRtA /
   visaṃdhinirākaraṇāya aurjityaṃ matam / patatprakarṣanirākaraṇāya rītiriṣṭā	visaMDi nirAkaraNAya Orjityam matam / patat prakarza nirAkaraNAya rItiH izwA
   / kliṣṭaparihārāya prasādo mataḥ / aślīlaparihārārthamuktiḥ svīkṛtā /	/ klizwa parihArAya prasAdaH mataH / aSlIla parihAra arTa muktiH svIkRtA /
